sign](https://www.cosmopolitan.com/sex-love/a23745601/zodiac-signs-compatibility/), there are pros and cons. One major pro: They understand you like no one else can. And one huge con: Together, your faults are multiplied and magnified. Both those facts are extra true for a [Scorpio/Scorpio couple](https://www.cosmopolitan.com/sex-love/a62707580/scorpio-compatibility-zodiac-signs/).\n\n[Scorpio](https://www.cosmopolitan.com/lifestyle/a33383019/scorpio-personality-traits/) is maybe \\*the\\* most intense sign of the zodiac. They’re all extremes—they either love you or hate you, they either keep everything secret or are uncomfortably wide-open about everything, they either approach the world with pragmatism and practicality or are totally melodramatic…sometimes all in the same day. When two Scorpios date each other, they’re both in for a wild ride. [Water](https://www.cosmopolitan.com/lifestyle/a32816867/water-signs-astrology/)\n\n**Modality:** [Fixed](https://www.cosmopolitan.com/lifestyle/a32131928/fixed-signs-astrology/)\n\n[**Ruler**](https://www.cosmopolitan.com/lifestyle/a30027024/astrology-zodiac-sign-ruling-planets/) **:** Mars Gabrielle Union, Tracee Ellis Ross, SZA, Ryan Reynolds, Ciara, Frank Ocean, Matthew McConaughey, Kris Jenner, Emma Stone, Leonardo DiCaprio\n\n## **Scorpio Personality Traits**\n\nYou’ve probably heard a little [something scary about Scorpio’s personality](https://www.cosmopolitan.com/lifestyle/a34315345/why-do-people-hate-scorpios/). They have intense emotions, they hold grudges for life, they’re secretive and mysterious, etc. All this is true, but Scorpios also have a soft side that they hide deep, deep down. They feel strong emotions and make loving, loyal friends and partners… if you can earn their trust, that is. (And you really have to earn it.)\n\n## **Scorpio and Scorpio: Friendship Compatibility**\n\nHere’s the thing about Scorpio: They don’t have all that many friends, and it’s 100% by choice. They prefer to keep most people at a distance. That doesn’t mean they’ll be cruel to you; they’ll be perfectly polite (unless you wrong them, that is) but they’ll also keep their guard up. Only a few of their nearest and dearest get to see Scorpio’s full selves, and odds are they’ve been BFFs with those lucky few since kindergarten. That said, a Scorpio can sometimes make space for a rare kindred spirit, and a fellow Scorpio might just fit the bill. You Might Be Wrong\n\nGetty/Margie Rischiotto\n\n## **Scorpio and Scorpio: Sexual Compatibility**\n\nIs it hot in here, or is it just two Scorpios flirting? Scorpio is \\*the\\* sign of sex, so yeah, obviously Scorpio and Scorpio are going to have amazing chemistry. In fact, their energy is so passionate and their emotions are so intense that a single makeout sesh can inspire them each to write books of erotic poetry and super-charge their spank banks. And when they actually get into bed together, well, wow is all I can say. These two can spend hours, days, even weeks exploring each other’s bodies and never get bored.\n\n## **Scorpio and Scorpio: Relationship Compatibility**\n\nSo, remember what I said about Scorpio and extremes? When things are good, this couple could basically star in their own romantic drama—the happily-ever-after part, like the safe-for-American-audiences-only kiss scene in _Pride and Prejudice_. And when things are bad, well, it’s basically a horror movie. Scorpio is one of the most stubborn signs of the zodiac, so neither person will admit they were wrong, back down, or give up the fight. Hopefully they have some mutable sign placements that can help them figure things out.\n\n## **Scorpio and Scorpio: Marriage Compatibility**\n\nYeah, everything I said about a Scorpio/Scorpio relationship is doubly true for a marriage. If they don’t want a quickie divorce, these two will need to learn how to talk through a disagreement because neither one will win in a standoff.\n\n## **Scorpio and Scorpio: Compatibility Summary**\n\nA Scorpio/Scorpio relationship is full of highs and lows—think romance, drama, passion, etc. For them to create something lasting, they’ll need to learn how to talk through fights, compromise, and forgive each other.\n\n## **Famous Scorpio and Scorpio Couples**\n\n_Together:_\n\n- Kendall Jenner and Devin Booker\n- Kris Jenner and Corey Gamble\n- Nick and Vanessa Lachey\n- Tracy These two were drawn together because of their undeniable magnetism. There is an electric current that seems to link two Scorpios together, and the passion they both have is undeniable. The potential downfall with a Scorpio-Scorpio relationship is that they are too similar, so the mind games they usually play with other signs won’t fly with their Scorpio partner. They both have the ability to see right through each other, down to each other’s soul. This fact either makes them either uncomfortable or very intrigued.\n\nIt is almost guaranteed that two Scorpios can become obsessed with one another and the way they make each other feel. Upon meeting, they probably felt like it was the first time someone understood them and could empathize with their feelings so well. They share a telepathic bond, and when either of them is not feeling well, the other immediately senses those frustrating feelings and will do anything to make them go away.\n\nScorpio is an all-or-nothing sign, so when these two love, they love with all of their hearts. And when they hate, they hate just as fiercely. This is why it is incredibly important for them both to beware in the midst of their arguments. They can both be very destructive with their words and may end up saying something they regret. As Scorpios, they are both very sensitive and do not forgive or forget easily, so if one or either of them harms each other verbally or emotionally, it may take a long time for them to get over such a setback.\n\nThe more positive these two are in this relationship, the greater of a chance that it will succeed. They feed off of each other’s energy, so they should keep it upbeat and transformative. There is a high chance that this relationship could become a lifelong commitment, such as marriage because they both are not the type to engage in casual or short-term relationships. They both are in it for the long-haul. If they both decide to break down their tough walls and trust each other with their deep, dark secrets, their link will strengthen and deepen even more.\n\nThis is a relationship that will stand out for the rest. It will be memorable both for your stormy arguments and your passionate make-up sessions. They will challenge, push, and pressure one another to be the best they possibly can. They both want to be number one in all that they do, and that includes having the number one relationship. If these two choose to let their positive attributes (strong intuition, empathy for those in need, passionate and determined nature, loyalty, faithfulness, and their depth of character) overcome their negative attributes, then this placement will be one of the strongest pillars for a long-lasting and joyful partnership.\n\n[![](https://i0.wp.com/scorpiomystique.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/03/signs-and-skymates-dosse-book-deck-journal.png?resize=1080%2C1080&ssl=1)](https://www.hachettebookgroup.com/titles/dosse-via-trenou/signs-skymates/9780762478019/#)\n\n## Want to learn more about how these zodiac placements are as friends, colleagues, family members, and frenemies?\n\n_Order ScorpioMystique founder Dossé-Via's new astrological compatibility book, [Signs & Skymates](http://dossevia.com/author)!_\n\n_This book revolutionizes the way we view love and relationships, through the lens of astrology and synastry._\n\n[Order Signs & Skymates](https://www.runningpress.com/titles/dosse-via-trenou/signs-skymates/9780762478019/)\n\n# 95 Comments\n\n01. ![Marie](https://secure.gravatar.com/avatar/b4d501a9395ada8b56aedd9a6e7dc14c?s=80&d=blank&r=g)\n\n\n\n Marie\n on September 29, 2014 at 8:50 am\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n Scorpio Mystique, I’ve been struggling to find any information on matching sun sign and rising sign relationships. When discussing a significant topic, each partner shares their initial thoughts, then acknowledges the emotions underlying those thoughts, and finally reveals the core needs or fears driving those emotions. Their identical astrological makeup creates friction in specific areas that require conscious navigation and mutual understanding.\n\n### Power Struggles and Control Issues\n\nPower dynamics emerge as a primary challenge in Scorpio-Scorpio relationships due to both partners' natural desire for control. These struggles manifest in daily decisions, from choosing restaurants to making significant life choices about careers or living arrangements. Two Scorpios locked in a battle for dominance create an atmosphere where compromise feels like surrender—a concept neither embraces easily.\n\nTheir fixed sign stubbornness compounds this issue, with disagreements often evolving into prolonged standoffs where neither partner willingly concedes ground. The relationship thrives when both recognize these patterns and establish clear domains of influence, allowing each partner to lead in different aspects of their shared life without feeling diminished.\n\n**⚠️ Relationship Alert:** Power struggles between two Scorpios can become particularly toxic if they evolve into emotional manipulation tactics. Be vigilant about using intimate knowledge as weapons during conflicts. Establish a relationship agreement early on that certain vulnerabilities remain protected even during heated arguments.\n\n### Handling Jealousy and Possessiveness\n\nJealousy surfaces intensely in Scorpio-Scorpio pairings as both partners experience this emotion with extraordinary depth. Their possessiveness stems from their profound emotional investment and fear of betrayal—emotions they recognize in each other. A casual conversation with an attractive colleague or an unexplained absence can trigger insecurities that spiral into interrogations or passive-aggressive behaviors.\n\nThis jealousy paradox—understanding yet struggling with the emotion—creates relationship tension unique to this zodiac pairing. Successful Scorpio couples address jealousy directly rather than letting it simmer, acknowledging these feelings without judgment while establishing trust through consistent transparency. They develop personalized boundaries that respect their security needs without suffocating their independence, striking a delicate balance between protective vigilance and stifling control.\n\n## Sexual Compatibility of Scorpio Man and Scorpio Woman\n\nThe sexual connection between a Scorpio man and Scorpio woman transcends physical pleasure, creating an experience that's deeply transformative and all-consuming. Their shared water element and fixed modality combine to produce a sexual relationship characterized by profound intensity and emotional depth.\n\n### Physical and Emotional Intimacy\n\nScorpio couples approach intimacy with unwavering commitment to authenticity. Physical encounters serve as extensions of their emotional connection, allowing both partners to express vulnerabilities they'd never reveal elsewhere. Their shared rulership by Mars infuses their sexual relationship with passion and endurance, while Pluto's influence drives their desire for psychological and spiritual merger through physical connection.\n\nTheir bedroom encounters feature an intuitive understanding of each other's desires, often anticipating needs before they're vocalized. This telepathic quality eliminates the awkwardness of communication about preferences, creating a seamless flow of giving and receiving pleasure. The Scorpio pair's exceptional eye contact during intimate moments strengthens their bond, as neither shies away from the vulnerability of being truly seen.\n\nPower exchanges occur naturally between these two intense individuals, with dominance and submission shifting fluidly depending on emotional needs and psychological dynamics. This creates a constantly evolving sexual landscape where both partners experience different facets of surrender and control. Their mutual understanding of power's erotic potential elevates their physical connection beyond purely physical satisfaction.\n\n### Building Trust in the Bedroom\n\nTrust develops progressively in their sexual relationship, allowing increasingly vulnerable expressions of desire. What begins as passionate encounters gradually transforms into a sanctuary where both partners explore deeper aspects of their sexuality without fear of judgment. This evolution mirrors their overall relationship development, moving from magnetic attraction to profound emotional intimacy.\n\nThe physical connection between Scorpio partners often has a spiritual dimension, with moments of transcendence during particularly intense encounters. Both recognize sex as a path to psychological transformation and healing, approaching intimacy with reverence for its potential to catalyze personal growth. These experiences create an unbreakable bond that continuously deepens with each encounter.\n\n**Intimacy Tip:** Create a ritual of emotional checking-in before intimate encounters. Taking five minutes to share current feelings, stresses, or desires helps Scorpio couples align emotionally before physical connection. This practice prevents external concerns from creating distance and deepens the transformative potential of their intimate moments.\n\n## Long-Term Potential for a Scorpio Couple\n\nA Scorpio-Scorpio relationship carries exceptional long-term potential, grounded in their shared emotional depth and commitment to authentic connection. These partnerships often evolve into lifelong bonds characterized by continuous growth, unwavering loyalty, and a rare level of intimacy that few other zodiac pairings achieve.\n\nThe cornerstone of their lasting potential lies in their mutual understanding of transformation. Both partners recognize that relationships, like individuals, must evolve or die—a perspective that allows them to navigate life's inevitable changes together rather than growing apart. Their shared water element provides an emotional fluidity that helps them adapt to life's challenges while maintaining their core connection.\n\nScorpio couples develop distinctive relationship patterns over time. Their initial passionate intensity gradually transforms into a profound emotional sanctuary where both partners feel completely seen and accepted. This evolution doesn't diminish their passion but rather enriches it with layers of meaning and history that accumulate over years together.\n\nThe fixed nature of their sign contributes significantly to their staying power. When two Scorpios commit, they bring remarkable determination to make the relationship work, viewing challenges as opportunities to deepen their bond rather than reasons to abandon it. This persistence creates a relationship that continuously strengthens through shared experiences and overcome obstacles.\n\nTheir mutual respect for emotional authenticity serves as a foundation for lasting happiness. Unlike partnerships where one person must compromise their emotional nature, Scorpio couples embrace each other's intensity, creating a relationship where both partners feel free to express their full emotional spectrum without judgment or restraint.\n\nTime typically resolves many initial power struggles as Scorpio couples establish balanced dynamics. Mature Scorpio relationships feature sophisticated power-sharing arrangements where each partner's strengths receive acknowledgment and their unique domains of influence gain respect. This evolution requires conscious effort but yields a partnership built on mutual respect rather than dominance.\n\nTheir shared values regarding loyalty and commitment provide stability through life's challenges. Both partners understand that true intimacy requires weathering difficult periods together, creating a resilience that strengthens their bond through financial hardships, health challenges, or external conflicts. Their unwavering support for each other during crises often becomes the cornerstone of their deepest connection.\n\nThe transformative potential of their relationship extends beyond the partnership itself, often catalyzing profound personal growth for both individuals. Long-term Scorpio couples frequently describe their relationship as the crucible through which they discovered their authentic selves—a testament to the alchemical nature of their connection.\n\n**Success Strategy:** Create a relationship vision board together that illustrates your shared goals and aspirations. Include images representing personal growth, mutual support, and the emotional sanctuary you're building together. Review and update it annually to ensure your relationship continues evolving rather than stagnating.\n\n## Famous Scorpio-Scorpio Couples\n\nLooking at real-world examples of Scorpio-Scorpio pairings provides insight into how this intense combination works in practice:\n\n**Katy Perry (October 25) & Orlando Bloom (January 13, Capricorn with Scorpio Moon)** While not a perfect Scorpio-Scorpio match by sun sign, Orlando's powerful Scorpio moon creates similar relationship dynamics. Their relationship demonstrates how two intense, emotionally complex individuals can create a stable partnership by honoring each other's depth while maintaining individuality.\n\n**Julia Roberts (October 28) & Matthew Perry (August 19, Leo with Scorpio Rising)** Another variation with Matthew's strong Scorpio ascendant influencing his presentation and relationship approach. Their friendship showcased the natural understanding and connection that occurs when Scorpio energy meets its match.\n\n**Ryan Gosling (November 12) & Rachel McAdams (November 17)** This famous former couple (both Scorpios) demonstrated both the passionate intensity and the challenges of a Scorpio-Scorpio relationship. Their on-again-off-again dynamic illustrated the transformative but sometimes volatile nature of this pairing.\n\n## Practical Advice for Scorpio-Scorpio Relationships\n\n### For Building Trust:\n\n- Practice radical transparency about your schedule and communications without demanding the same\n- Create a \"privacy with purpose\" agreement—respecting alone time without secrecy\n- Develop trust-building rituals like daily check-ins about emotional states\n\n### For Handling Intensity:\n\n- Establish a \"cooling off\" protocol for heated moments\n- Create code words to signal when emotional intensity is becoming overwhelming\n- Maintain individual friendships and activities to prevent emotional codependency\n\n### For Managing Power Dynamics:\n\n- Clearly define areas of relationship responsibility based on strengths\n- Practice taking turns leading in decision-making processes\n- Acknowledge and appreciate when your partner concedes in a disagreement\n\n### For Communication:\n\n- Schedule regular relationship check-ins to address issues before they escalate\n- Practice reflective listening techniques during difficult conversations\n- Develop non-verbal signals for emotional support in social situations\n\n### Common Challenges and Solutions\n\n| Challenge | Why It Happens | Solution |\n| --- | --- | --- |\n| Power Struggles | Both need control and resist vulnerability | Establish clear domains of authority and practice turn-taking with decisions |\n| Emotional Flooding | Intense feelings overwhelm rational thought | Create a \"time-out\" system with agreed follow-up time to continue discussions |\n| Mutual Suspicion | Projection of own capacity for secrecy | Build trust through consistent transparency about activities and communications |\n| Emotional Withdrawal | Self-protection during conflict | Develop a reconnection ritual for after disagreements to prevent prolonged distance |\n| Competitive Dynamics | Need to maintain psychological advantage | Reframe relationship as a team facing external challenges rather than internal opponents |\n| Revenge Impulses | Deep hurt triggers protective retaliation | Establish a \"no weapons of mass destruction\" agreement about fighting fairly |\n\nHave you experienced a Scorpio-Scorpio relationship? Keep reading for more info!\n\n## Things You Should Know\n\n- Scorpios’ passion, sensuality, and emotional sensitivity make them a natural match.\n- Slow to trust, they are intensely loyal once they’ve opened up, but their instinct for self-preservation makes them reluctant to forgive betrayal.\n- These two will thrive in a relationship as long as they learn to trust and become less stubborn and competitive.\n\n## Steps\n\nSection 1 of 6:\n\n### Scorpio & Scorpio Compatibility Overview\n\n[![PDF download](https://www.wikihow.com/extensions/wikihow/socialstamp/images/icon-pdf.svg)Download Article](https://www.wikihow.com/Scorpio-Man-Scorpio-Woman#)\n\n1. [![Scorpios make a passionate, well-matched pair.](https://www.wikihow.com/images/thumb/3/38/Scorpio-Man-Scorpio-Woman-Step-1.jpg/v4-460px-Scorpio-Man-Scorpio-Woman-Step-1.jpg)](https://www.wikihow.com/Scorpio-Man-Scorpio-Woman#/Image:Scorpio-Man-Scorpio-Woman-Step-1.jpg)\n\n**Scorpios make a passionate, well-matched pair.** A Scorpio man and a Scorpio woman will bring equal amounts of passion, emotional sensitivity, introspection, sensuality, and loyalty to a relationship. And did we mention the sex? These two just need to learn to trust one another—not something that comes naturally to them—and their relationship will thrive.\n\n\n- Scorpios are naturally a bit mistrustful and secretive, but this means that once their loyalty is won, they don’t relinquish it easily. These two are capable of soulmate-level intimacy—if only they can learn to rely on one another, share their secrets, and let down their guard.\n\nAdvertisement\n\nSection 2 of 6:\n\n### Scorpio & Scorpio Sexual Compatibility\n\n[![PDF download](https://www.wikihow.com/extensions/wikihow/socialstamp/images/icon-pdf.svg)Download Article](https://www.wikihow.com/Scorpio-Man-Scorpio-Woman#)\n\n1. [![Sex between Scorpios is hot, hot, hot.](https://www.wikihow.com/images/thumb/2/26/Scorpio-Man-Scorpio-Woman-Step-2.jpg/v4-460px-Scorpio-Man-Scorpio-Woman-Step-2.jpg)](https://www.wikihow.com/Scorpio-Man-Scorpio-Woman#/Image:Scorpio-Man-Scorpio-Woman-Step-2.jpg)\n\n**Sex between Scorpios is hot, hot, hot.** Each sign in the zodiac rules over a different body part, and it’ll come as no surprise that Scorpio rules over the genitals.[\\[1\\]](https://www.wikihow.com/Scorpio-Man-Scorpio-Woman#_note-1)XResearch source Scorpios are deeply passionate. They infuse every moment of their day with sensuality, making it almost an intrinsic part of their day-to-day life—like air. In a relationship, two Scorpios will appreciate one another’s equal commitment to and understanding of the value of a thriving sex life.[\\[2\\]](https://www.wikihow.com/Scorpio-Man-Scorpio-Woman#_note-2)X [Expert Source](https://www.wikihow.com/wikiHow:Delivering-a-Trustworthy-Experience) [![Angel Eyedealism](https://www.wikihow.com/images/thumb/0/02/Angel_Eyedealism.png/-crop-100-100-100px-Angel_Eyedealism.png)Angel Eyedealism\\\\\n\\\\\nAstrologer & Performance Artist](https://www.wikihow.com/Author/Angel-Eyedealism) Expert Interview\n\n- Scorpios aren’t afraid to get creative in the sack. Since they both value keeping their sex life alive and hopping, they’ll make efforts to spice things up in the bedroom and make sure their partner is satisfied.\n\nSection 3 of 6:\n\n### Scorpio & Scorpio Emotional Compatibility\n\n[![PDF download](https://www.wikihow.com/extensions/wikihow/socialstamp/images/icon-pdf.svg)Download Article](https://www.wikihow.com/Scorpio-Man-Scorpio-Woman#)\n\n1. [![As water signs, these two share a strong emotional connection.](https://www.wikihow.com/images/thumb/a/ae/Scorpio-Man-Scorpio-Woman-Step-3.jpg/v4-460px-Scorpio-Man-Scorpio-Woman-Step-3.jpg)](https://www.wikihow.com/Scorpio-Man-Scorpio-Woman#/Image:Scorpio-Man-Scorpio-Woman-Step-3.jpg)\n\n**As water signs, these two share a strong emotional connection.** They are both deeply empathetic people and are likely to be twin flames. Slow to trust, intimacy may not come quickly, but when it does, it comes naturally.[\\[3\\]](https://www.wikihow.com/Scorpio-Man-Scorpio-Woman#_note-3)X [Expert Source](https://www.wikihow.com/wikiHow:Delivering-a-Trustworthy-Experience) [![Jessica Lanyadoo](https://www.wikihow.com/images/thumb/1/1e/Jessica_Lanyadoo_.png/-crop-100-100-100px-Jessica_Lanyadoo_.png)Jessica Lanyadoo\\\\\n\\\\\nAstrologer & Psychic Medium](https://www.wikihow.com/Author/Jessica-Lanyadoo) Expert Interview They are capable of plumbing one another’s emotional depths, and they love to do so: these two signs are on an emotional wavelength other signs can’t even contemplate. It's almost as if they're reading one another's minds at times.[\\[4\\]](https://www.wikihow.com/Scorpio-Man-Scorpio-Woman#_note-4)XResearch source\n\n- Because they’re so secretive, sharing secrets with one another is the best way to cultivate a strong emotional connection. Scorpios consider it an honor to be entrusted with another person’s private secrets, especially another Scorpio.[\\[5\\]](https://www.wikihow.com/Scorpio-Man-Scorpio-Woman#_note-5)X [Expert Source](https://www.wikihow.com/wikiHow:Delivering-a-Trustworthy-Experience) [![Angel Eyedealism](https://www.wikihow.com/images/thumb/0/02/Angel_Eyedealism.png/-crop-100-100-100px-Angel_Eyedealism.png)Angel Eyedealism\\\\\n\\\\\nAstrologer & Performance Artist](https://www.wikihow.com/Author/Angel-Eyedealism) Expert Interview\n- Since Scorpios can be slow to trust, it’s vital that they be honest with one another to make this a compatible match.\n\nTELL US WHAT YOU THINK\n\nWhich element of compatibility is most important to you in a relationship?\n\nSexual compatibility.\n\n\nEmotional compatibility.\n\n\nCommunication compatibility.\n\n\nTrust compatibility.\n\n\n1805 total votes. [![They’re stubborn but sensitive communicators.](https://www.wikihow.com/images/thumb/9/9e/Scorpio-Man-Scorpio-Woman-Step-4.jpg/v4-460px-Scorpio-Man-Scorpio-Woman-Step-4.jpg)](https://www.wikihow.com/Scorpio-Man-Scorpio-Woman#/Image:Scorpio-Man-Scorpio-Woman-Step-4.jpg)\n\n**They’re stubborn but sensitive communicators.** Because Scorpio is ruled by the dark and mysterious Pluto, they may be slow to share their feelings. And since they’re _also_ ruled by the aggressive Mars and are fixed signs, they may sometimes be overly stubborn or refuse to give ground in an argument.[\\[6\\]](https://www.wikihow.com/Scorpio-Man-Scorpio-Woman#_note-6)X [Expert Source](https://www.wikihow.com/wikiHow:Delivering-a-Trustworthy-Experience) [![Jessica Lanyadoo](https://www.wikihow.com/images/thumb/1/1e/Jessica_Lanyadoo_.png/-crop-100-100-100px-Jessica_Lanyadoo_.png)Jessica Lanyadoo\\\\\n\\\\\nAstrologer & Psychic Medium](https://www.wikihow.com/Author/Jessica-Lanyadoo) Expert Interview However, their emotional intelligence and sensitivity, as well as their strong sense of devotion, mean that they’re usually invested in resolving disagreements with their partner.\n\n\n- It may help two Scorpios who are arguing to intentionally slow down and take breaks often. Since they’re both Scorpios, they’re likely to understand one another’s emotional and communication weaknesses and to have some grace for those weaknesses.\n\nSection 5 of 6:\n\n### Scorpio & Scorpio Values\n\n[![PDF download](https://www.wikihow.com/extensions/wikihow/socialstamp/images/icon-pdf.svg)Download Article](https://www.wikihow.com/Scorpio-Man-Scorpio-Woman#)\n\n1. [![Scorpios value loyalty, making betrayal a major offense.](https://www.wikihow.com/images/thumb/6/69/Scorpio-Man-Scorpio-Woman-Step-5.jpg/v4-460px-Scorpio-Man-Scorpio-Woman-Step-5.jpg)](https://www.wikihow.com/Scorpio-Man-Scorpio-Woman#/Image:Scorpio-Man-Scorpio-Woman-Step-5.jpg)\n\n**Scorpios value loyalty, making betrayal a major offense.** Because Scorpios are so guarded and mysterious, when they devote themselves to something or someone, they expect loyalty and devotion in return. They’re emotionally intelligent enough to understand the reasons behind betrayal, but as the sign with the rawest nerves in the zodiac, they’re unlikely to forgive disloyalty.\n\n\n- Represented by the scorpion, a Scorpio’s intensity can make them “scary” to other signs, but their cold, dark, intense personas are really just there to defend the ultra-tender hearts underneath.[\\[7\\]](https://www.wikihow.com/Scorpio-Man-Scorpio-Woman#_note-7)X [Expert Source](https://www.wikihow.com/wikiHow:Delivering-a-Trustworthy-Experience) [![Jessica Lanyadoo](https://www.wikihow.com/images/thumb/1/1e/Jessica_Lanyadoo_.png/-crop-100-100-100px-Jessica_Lanyadoo_.png)Jessica Lanyadoo\\\\\n\\\\\nAstrologer & Psychic Medium](https://www.wikihow.com/Author/Jessica-Lanyadoo) Expert Interview\n- **Reader Poll:** We asked 845 wikiHow readers who are Scorpios, and **65%** of them agreed that their biggest dealbreaker is **lying**. [\\[Take Poll\\]](https://www.wikihow.com/Best-Match-for-Scorpio-Man#reader_poll_1765) So to avoid feelings of betrayal in a Scorpio-Scorpio relationship, both partners should always tell the truth—even when it's hard.\n\nAdvertisement\n\nSection 6 of 6:\n\n### Scorpio & Scorpio Potential Challenges\n\n[![PDF download](https://www.wikihow.com/extensions/wikihow/socialstamp/images/icon-pdf.svg)Download Article](https://www.wikihow.com/Scorpio-Man-Scorpio-Woman#)\n\n1. [![Two Scorpios may...](https://www.wikihow.com/images/thumb/b/be/Scorpio-Man-Scorpio-Woman-Step-6.jpg/v4-460px-Scorpio-Man-Scorpio-Woman-Step-6.jpg)](https://www.wikihow.com/Scorpio-Man-Scorpio-Woman#/Image:Scorpio-Man-Scorpio-Woman-Step-6.jpg)\n\n**Two Scorpios may struggle to [**trust**](https://www.wikihow.com/Trust \"Trust\") one another.** Scorpios in love share an intense emotional connection verging on telepathy. They can sense what the other feels and needs, and their loyalty and dedication make them a natural pair. They just need to be sure to abandon their instinct for self-preservation around one another—the instinct that makes them prone to secrecy and stubbornness. A relationship won’t last without vulnerability, trust, and flexibility.\n\n\n- Scorpios in love may also struggle if they become competitive with one another—say, if they’re in the same career field or have the same hobby. As long as they maintain some independence within their relationship, they may [avoid competition](https://www.wikihow.com/Stop-Being-Competitive \"Stop Being Competitive\") with each other.\n\n## sign](https://www.cosmopolitan.com/sex-love/a23745601/zodiac-signs-compatibility/), there are pros and cons. One major pro: They understand you like no one else can. And one huge con: Together, your faults are multiplied and magnified. Both those facts are extra true for a [Scorpio/Scorpio couple](https://www.cosmopolitan.com/sex-love/a62707580/scorpio-compatibility-zodiac-signs/).\n\n[Scorpio](https://www.cosmopolitan.com/lifestyle/a33383019/scorpio-personality-traits/) is maybe \\*the\\* most intense sign of the zodiac. They’re all extremes—they either love you or hate you, they either keep everything secret or are uncomfortably wide-open about everything, they either approach the world with pragmatism and practicality or are totally melodramatic…sometimes all in the same day. When two Scorpios date each other, they’re both in for a wild ride. [Water](https://www.cosmopolitan.com/lifestyle/a32816867/water-signs-astrology/)\n\n**Modality:** [Fixed](https://www.cosmopolitan.com/lifestyle/a32131928/fixed-signs-astrology/)\n\n[**Ruler**](https://www.cosmopolitan.com/lifestyle/a30027024/astrology-zodiac-sign-ruling-planets/) **:** Mars Gabrielle Union, Tracee Ellis Ross, SZA, Ryan Reynolds, Ciara, Frank Ocean, Matthew McConaughey, Kris Jenner, Emma Stone, Leonardo DiCaprio\n\n## **Scorpio Personality Traits**\n\nYou’ve probably heard a little [something scary about Scorpio’s personality](https://www.cosmopolitan.com/lifestyle/a34315345/why-do-people-hate-scorpios/). They have intense emotions, they hold grudges for life, they’re secretive and mysterious, etc. All this is true, but Scorpios also have a soft side that they hide deep, deep down. They feel strong emotions and make loving, loyal friends and partners… if you can earn their trust, that is. (And you really have to earn it.)\n\n## **Scorpio and Scorpio: Friendship Compatibility**\n\nHere’s the thing about Scorpio: They don’t have all that many friends, and it’s 100% by choice. They prefer to keep most people at a distance. That doesn’t mean they’ll be cruel to you; they’ll be perfectly polite (unless you wrong them, that is) but they’ll also keep their guard up. Only a few of their nearest and dearest get to see Scorpio’s full selves, and odds are they’ve been BFFs with those lucky few since kindergarten. That said, a Scorpio can sometimes make space for a rare kindred spirit, and a fellow Scorpio might just fit the bill. You Might Be Wrong\n\nGetty/Margie Rischiotto\n\n## **Scorpio and Scorpio: Sexual Compatibility**\n\nIs it hot in here, or is it just two Scorpios flirting? Scorpio is \\*the\\* sign of sex, so yeah, obviously Scorpio and Scorpio are going to have amazing chemistry. In fact, their energy is so passionate and their emotions are so intense that a single makeout sesh can inspire them each to write books of erotic poetry and super-charge their spank banks. And when they actually get into bed together, well, wow is all I can say. These two can spend hours, days, even weeks exploring each other’s bodies and never get bored.\n\n## **Scorpio and Scorpio: Relationship Compatibility**\n\nSo, remember what I said about Scorpio and extremes? When things are good, this couple could basically star in their own romantic drama—the happily-ever-after part, like the safe-for-American-audiences-only kiss scene in _Pride and Prejudice_. And when things are bad, well, it’s basically a horror movie. Scorpio is one of the most stubborn signs of the zodiac, so neither person will admit they were wrong, back down, or give up the fight. Hopefully they have some mutable sign placements that can help them figure things out.\n\n## **Scorpio and Scorpio: Marriage Compatibility**\n\nYeah, everything I said about a Scorpio/Scorpio relationship is doubly true for a marriage. If they don’t want a quickie divorce, these two will need to learn how to talk through a disagreement because neither one will win in a standoff.\n\n## **Scorpio and Scorpio: Compatibility Summary**\n\nA Scorpio/Scorpio relationship is full of highs and lows—think romance, drama, passion, etc. For them to create something lasting, they’ll need to learn how to talk through fights, compromise, and forgive each other.\n\n## **Famous Scorpio and Scorpio Couples**\n\n_Together:_\n\n- Kendall Jenner and Devin Booker\n- Kris Jenner and Corey Gamble\n- Nick and Vanessa Lachey\n- Tracy ny way, their contact can become truly unpleasant and turn to arguing, dismissal of anything said, or in one word – disrespect. When they start a battle against each other, it cannot seem to stop, until one of them is beaten “dead” and there is nothing more that can be done for them to get back in the game. If they see each other as adversaries, they will sting each other for victory, meaning they will do whatever it takes to win. If they distance themselves from a situation, they might realize that none of them actually endangers the other. To find mutual understanding, they need to lead separate lives and give each other enough room to do so.\n\n### 70%\n\n## Emotions\n\n![Scorpio And Scorpio Emotions](https://www.zodiacsign.com/images/scorpio_emotions_compatibility_-min.jpg)\n\n[Scorpio](https://www.zodiacsign.com/zodiac-signs/scorpio/) is a Water sign and represents all dismissed emotions we don’t want to deal with. This makes representatives of this sign turned to the dark emotional issues and this is something they will both understand in each other. The problem with Scorpio is in its battle with the Moon and the fact that emotions aren’t approved here. This can make them both intolerant for weakness, rough in their approach to one another and too judgmental toward each other’s emotional needs, even though they both actually share the same needs.\n\nThey will both be faced with emotions they don’t want to deal with, simply because that is their individual role in other people’s lives. This could lead to numerous conflicts, but it could also be the base for incredible personal evolution of each partner, and an opportunity to be with someone who truly understands the depth of their hearts. The best way for them to approach this relationship is through deepest emotional acceptance and the tolerance for incredible difference in character, even though they are, strangely, the same.\n\n### 55%\n\n## Values\n\n![Scorpio And Scorpio Values](https://www.zodiacsign.com/images/scorpio_values_compatibility_-min.jpg)\n\nThe problem with things they value is in the illusion of value they both share. They will value rationality and emotional maturity, but those are things none of them can actually deliver all the time. They belong to the element of Water and are deeply emotional, while valuing each other’s lack of emotion, shown at the beginning of their relationship. They do value similar things, but they are not entirely rational or realistic in their choices. This makes them susceptible to judging their own reflection in one another.\n\n### 90%\n\n## Shared Activities\n\n![Scorpio And Scorpio Shared Activities](https://www.zodiacsign.com/images/scorpio_activities_compatibility_-min.jpg)\n\nThey won’t have a hard time discussing or agreeing on where to go and what to do together, but their choices might not make them happy. Again, this is about the balance they both seek, needing a partner of opposite character and choices. Their contact could lead them to all the dark places, as they play out situations they couldn’t play out with anyone else. Even though they will feel sad and dried out most of the time, as two members of fixed quality, they could hold on to each other for a long time. The more time they spend together, the less energy they might have, for there is a silent, inner battle in both of them that drains it out of their systems.\n\n### 75%\n\n## Summary\n\nScorpio and Scorpio have this tendency to bring out the worst in each other. Even though they can share the deepest understanding known to the entire zodiac, they can also get too dark and depressed together, sinking into their pool of unresolved emotions. Their emotional understanding is something worth cherishing, if they are both open for their own feelings and accept their own inner needs.\n\n### 66%\n\n![Iva Vucinic](https://www.zodiacsign.com/images/iva-v-min.png)\n\n[Iva Vucinic](https://www.zodiacsign.com/author/iva-vucinic/) is a highly regarded professional astrologer and psychologist. But I think as long as you and your man have an understanding the relationship will be great because Scorpios are know to be very stubborn and emotional people at times.\n\nI hope this helps you! 😊\n\n1 Upvote\n\n* * *\n\nAn\n\nPosted at Fri, Jul 21 2017\n\nI'm a scorpio and my SO is a cancer. water signs are the BEST!!!\n\n0 Upvote\n\n* * *\n\nHa\n\nPosted at Tue, Jul 04 2017\n\nWhat does a horoscope actually have to do with someone's character\n\n0 Upvote\n\nHa\n\nHannah • Tue, Jul 04 2017\n\nI don't even know my boyfriend's sign\n\n* * *\n\n[Please Help](https://glowing.com/community/topic/2409525/please-help) <\\- Previous\n\n[TMI pic- Is this fertile CM or...](https://glowing.com/community/topic/2410148/tmi-pic-is-this-fertile-cm-orrrr-something-else) Next ->\n\n* * *\n\n## Related Articles\n\n![Can You Get Pregnant from Precum (And What Are the Chances of It Happening)?](https://glowcontent.wpengine.com/wp-content/uploads/2025/03/what-are-the-chances-of-getting-pregnant-from-precum.avif)Sex\n\n[**Can You Get Pregnant from Precum (And What Are the Chances of It Happening)?**](https://glowing.com/resources/getting-pregnant/what-are-the-chances-of-getting-pregnant-from-precum)\n\n* * *\n\nMedically Reviewed by: [Monica Lee, MD, FACOG](https://glowcontent.wpengine.com/person/monica-lee)","headings":{"h1":[],"h2":[],"h3":["Can You Get Pregnant from Precum (And What Are the Chances of It Happening)?"]},"wordCount":1208,"metaDescription":"My husband and I are both scorpios. Stina holds an Ordained Minister License from The International Metaphysical Ministry University Seminary.\n\n\n\nThis article has been viewed 61,702 times.\n\n\n\nScorpios are known as one of the most intense, sensual, and mysterious astrological signs, and when you get a Scorpio man and a Scorpio woman together, that’s two times the intensity, sensuality, and mystery. Despite their tendency toward secrecy and distrust, two Scorpios really make a great match! In this article, we’ve outlined what to expect from a Scorpio-Scorpio relationship, including sexual and emotional compatibility, communication habits, shared values, and potential challenges they may face. Keep reading for more info!\n\n## Things You Should Know\n\n- Scorpios’ passion, sensuality, and emotional sensitivity make them a natural match.\n- Slow to trust, they are intensely loyal once they’ve opened up, but their instinct for self-preservation makes them reluctant to forgive betrayal.\n- These two will thrive in a relationship as long as they learn to trust and become less stubborn and competitive.\n\n## Steps\n\nSection 1 of 6:\n\n### Scorpio & Scorpio Compatibility Overview\n\n[![PDF download](https://www.wikihow.com/extensions/wikihow/socialstamp/images/icon-pdf.svg)Download Article](https://www.wikihow.com/Scorpio-Man-Scorpio-Woman#)\n\n1. [![Scorpios make a passionate, well-matched pair.](https://www.wikihow.com/images/thumb/3/38/Scorpio-Man-Scorpio-Woman-Step-1.jpg/v4-460px-Scorpio-Man-Scorpio-Woman-Step-1.jpg)](https://www.wikihow.com/Scorpio-Man-Scorpio-Woman#/Image:Scorpio-Man-Scorpio-Woman-Step-1.jpg)\n\n**Scorpios make a passionate, well-matched pair.** A Scorpio man and a Scorpio woman will bring equal amounts of passion, emotional sensitivity, introspection, sensuality, and loyalty to a relationship. And did we mention the sex? These two just need to learn to trust one another—not something that comes naturally to them—and their relationship will thrive.\n\n\n- Scorpios are naturally a bit mistrustful and secretive, but this means that once their loyalty is won, they don’t relinquish it easily. These two are capable of soulmate-level intimacy—if only they can learn to rely on one another, share their secrets, and let down their guard.\n\nAdvertisement\n\nSection 2 of 6:\n\n### Scorpio & Scorpio Sexual Compatibility\n\n[![PDF download](https://www.wikihow.com/extensions/wikihow/socialstamp/images/icon-pdf.svg)Download Article](https://www.wikihow.com/Scorpio-Man-Scorpio-Woman#)\n\n1. [![Sex between Scorpios is hot, hot, hot.](https://www.wikihow.com/images/thumb/2/26/Scorpio-Man-Scorpio-Woman-Step-2.jpg/v4-460px-Scorpio-Man-Scorpio-Woman-Step-2.jpg)](https://www.wikihow.com/Scorpio-Man-Scorpio-Woman#/Image:Scorpio-Man-Scorpio-Woman-Step-2.jpg)\n\n**Sex between Scorpios is hot, hot, hot.** Each sign in the zodiac rules over a different body part, and it’ll come as no surprise that Scorpio rules over the genitals.[\\[1\\]](https://www.wikihow.com/Scorpio-Man-Scorpio-Woman#_note-1)XResearch source Scorpios are deeply passionate. They infuse every moment of their day with sensuality, making it almost an intrinsic part of their day-to-day life—like air. In a relationship, two Scorpios will appreciate one another’s equal commitment to and understanding of the value of a thriving sex life.[\\[2\\]](https://www.wikihow.com/Scorpio-Man-Scorpio-Woman#_note-2)X [Expert Source](https://www.wikihow.com/wikiHow:Delivering-a-Trustworthy-Experience) [![Angel Eyedealism](https://www.wikihow.com/images/thumb/0/02/Angel_Eyedealism.png/-crop-100-100-100px-Angel_Eyedealism.png)Angel Eyedealism\\\\\n\\\\\nAstrologer & Performance Artist](https://www.wikihow.com/Author/Angel-Eyedealism) Expert Interview\n\n- Scorpios aren’t afraid to get creative in the sack. Since they both value keeping their sex life alive and hopping, they’ll make efforts to spice things up in the bedroom and make sure their partner is satisfied.\n\nSection 3 of 6:\n\n### Scorpio & Scorpio Emotional Compatibility\n\n[![PDF download](https://www.wikihow.com/extensions/wikihow/socialstamp/images/icon-pdf.svg)Download Article](https://www.wikihow.com/Scorpio-Man-Scorpio-Woman#)\n\n1. [![As water signs, these two share a strong emotional connection.](https://www.wikihow.com/images/thumb/a/ae/Scorpio-Man-Scorpio-Woman-Step-3.jpg/v4-460px-Scorpio-Man-Scorpio-Woman-Step-3.jpg)](https://www.wikihow.com/Scorpio-Man-Scorpio-Woman#/Image:Scorpio-Man-Scorpio-Woman-Step-3.jpg)\n\n**As water signs, these two share a strong emotional connection.** They are both deeply empathetic people and are likely to be twin flames. Slow to trust, intimacy may not come quickly, but when it does, it comes naturally.[\\[3\\]](https://www.wikihow.com/Scorpio-Man-Scorpio-Woman#_note-3)X [Expert Source](https://www.wikihow.com/wikiHow:Delivering-a-Trustworthy-Experience) [![Jessica Lanyadoo](https://www.wikihow.com/images/thumb/1/1e/Jessica_Lanyadoo_.png/-crop-100-100-100px-Jessica_Lanyadoo_.png)Jessica Lanyadoo\\\\\n\\\\\nAstrologer & Psychic Medium](https://www.wikihow.com/Author/Jessica-Lanyadoo) Expert Interview They are capable of plumbing one another’s emotional depths, and they love to do so: these two signs are on an emotional wavelength other signs can’t even contemplate. It's almost as if they're reading one another's minds at times.[\\[4\\]](https://www.wikihow.com/Scorpio-Man-Scorpio-Woman#_note-4)XResearch source\n\n- Because they’re so secretive, sharing secrets with one another is the best way to cultivate a strong emotional connection. Scorpios consider it an honor to be entrusted with another person’s private secrets, especially another Scorpio.[\\[5\\]](https://www.wikihow.com/Scorpio-Man-Scorpio-Woman#_note-5)X [Expert Source](https://www.wikihow.com/wikiHow:Delivering-a-Trustworthy-Experience) [![Angel Eyedealism](https://www.wikihow.com/images/thumb/0/02/Angel_Eyedealism.png/-crop-100-100-100px-Angel_Eyedealism.png)Angel Eyedealism\\\\\n\\\\\nAstrologer & Performance Artist](https://www.wikihow.com/Author/Angel-Eyedealism) Expert Interview\n- Since Scorpios can be slow to trust, it’s vital that they be honest with one another to make this a compatible match.\n\nTELL US WHAT YOU THINK\n\nWhich element of compatibility is most important to you in a relationship?\n\nSexual compatibility.\n\n\nEmotional compatibility.\n\n\nCommunication compatibility.\n\n\nTrust compatibility.\n\n\n1805 total votes. [![They’re stubborn but sensitive communicators.](https://www.wikihow.com/images/thumb/9/9e/Scorpio-Man-Scorpio-Woman-Step-4.jpg/v4-460px-Scorpio-Man-Scorpio-Woman-Step-4.jpg)](https://www.wikihow.com/Scorpio-Man-Scorpio-Woman#/Image:Scorpio-Man-Scorpio-Woman-Step-4.jpg)\n\n**They’re stubborn but sensitive communicators.** Because Scorpio is ruled by the dark and mysterious Pluto, they may be slow to share their feelings. And since they’re _also_ ruled by the aggressive Mars and are fixed signs, they may sometimes be overly stubborn or refuse to give ground in an argument.[\\[6\\]](https://www.wikihow.com/Scorpio-Man-Scorpio-Woman#_note-6)X [Expert Source](https://www.wikihow.com/wikiHow:Delivering-a-Trustworthy-Experience) [![Jessica Lanyadoo](https://www.wikihow.com/images/thumb/1/1e/Jessica_Lanyadoo_.png/-crop-100-100-100px-Jessica_Lanyadoo_.png)Jessica Lanyadoo\\\\\n\\\\\nAstrologer & Psychic Medium](https://www.wikihow.com/Author/Jessica-Lanyadoo) Expert Interview However, their emotional intelligence and sensitivity, as well as their strong sense of devotion, mean that they’re usually invested in resolving disagreements with their partner.\n\n\n- It may help two Scorpios who are arguing to intentionally slow down and take breaks often. Since they’re both Scorpios, they’re likely to understand one another’s emotional and communication weaknesses and to have some grace for those weaknesses.\n\nSection 5 of 6:\n\n### Scorpio & Scorpio Values\n\n[![PDF download](https://www.wikihow.com/extensions/wikihow/socialstamp/images/icon-pdf.svg)Download Article](https://www.wikihow.com/Scorpio-Man-Scorpio-Woman#)\n\n1. [![Scorpios value loyalty, making betrayal a major offense.](https://www.wikihow.com/images/thumb/6/69/Scorpio-Man-Scorpio-Woman-Step-5.jpg/v4-460px-Scorpio-Man-Scorpio-Woman-Step-5.jpg)](https://www.wikihow.com/Scorpio-Man-Scorpio-Woman#/Image:Scorpio-Man-Scorpio-Woman-Step-5.jpg)\n\n**Scorpios value loyalty, making betrayal a major offense.** Because Scorpios are so guarded and mysterious, when they devote themselves to something or someone, they expect loyalty and devotion in return. They’re emotionally intelligent enough to understand the reasons behind betrayal, but as the sign with the rawest nerves in the zodiac, they’re unlikely to forgive disloyalty.\n\n\n- Represented by the scorpion, a Scorpio’s intensity can make them “scary” to other signs, but their cold, dark, intense personas are really just there to defend the ultra-tender hearts underneath.[\\[7\\]](https://www.wikihow.com/Scorpio-Man-Scorpio-Woman#_note-7)X [Expert Source](https://www.wikihow.com/wikiHow:Delivering-a-Trustworthy-Experience) [![Jessica Lanyadoo](https://www.wikihow.com/images/thumb/1/1e/Jessica_Lanyadoo_.png/-crop-100-100-100px-Jessica_Lanyadoo_.png)Jessica Lanyadoo\\\\\n\\\\\nAstrologer & Psychic Medium](https://www.wikihow.com/Author/Jessica-Lanyadoo) Expert Interview\n- **Reader Poll:** We asked 845 wikiHow readers who are Scorpios, and **65%** of them agreed that their biggest dealbreaker is **lying**. [\\[Take Poll\\]](https://www.wikihow.com/Best-Match-for-Scorpio-Man#reader_poll_1765) So to avoid feelings of betrayal in a Scorpio-Scorpio relationship, both partners should always tell the truth—even when it's hard.\n\nAdvertisement\n\nSection 6 of 6:\n\n### Scorpio & Scorpio Potential Challenges\n\n[![PDF download](https://www.wikihow.com/extensions/wikihow/socialstamp/images/icon-pdf.svg)Download Article](https://www.wikihow.com/Scorpio-Man-Scorpio-Woman#)\n\n1. [![Two Scorpios may...](https://www.wikihow.com/images/thumb/b/be/Scorpio-Man-Scorpio-Woman-Step-6.jpg/v4-460px-Scorpio-Man-Scorpio-Woman-Step-6.jpg)](https://www.wikihow.com/Scorpio-Man-Scorpio-Woman#/Image:Scorpio-Man-Scorpio-Woman-Step-6.jpg)\n\n**Two Scorpios may struggle to [**trust**](https://www.wikihow.com/Trust \"Trust\") one another.** Scorpios in love
2026-02-05 12:06:57.16

share an intense emotional connection verging on telepathy. They can sense what the other feels and needs, and their loyalty and dedication make them a natural pair. They just need to be sure to abandon their instinct for self-preservation around one another—the instinct that makes them prone to secrecy and stubbornness. A relationship won’t last without vulnerability, trust, and flexibility.\n\n\n- Scorpios in love may also struggle if they become competitive with one another—say, if they’re in the same career field or have the same hobby. As long as they maintain some independence within their relationship, they may [avoid competition](https://www.wikihow.com/Stop-Being-Competitive \"Stop Being Competitive\") with each other.\n\n## Their connection often feels predestined, with an almost telepathic understanding flowing between them. However, this mirror-like compatibility comes with challenges – when two equally powerful forces collide, power struggles and intense jealousy can emerge.\n\n**Real-Life Insight:** \"Meeting another Scorpio was like looking into an emotional mirror,\" shares Michael, a financial analyst. \"Sophia and I connected instantly on a level I'd never experienced before. This powerful connection stems from their shared water element and planetary rulers, creating an almost supernatural bond that's rarely experienced with other zodiac pairings.\n\nTheir connection operates on multiple levels simultaneously—physical, emotional, and psychic. Both partners intuitively understand each other's deepest desires and motivations without needing explicit communication. This telepathic understanding creates a sense of \"coming home\" when they're together, as if they've known each other across multiple lifetimes.\n\nThe Scorpio-Scorpio connection is characterized by:\n\n- Instant recognition of something familiar yet mysterious in each other\n- Unspoken understanding of emotional needs and boundaries\n- Shared intensity that others often find overwhelming\n- Complete emotional nakedness that feels both terrifying and liberating\n\nTheir magnetism defies simple explanation—it's a powerful gravitational pull that both Scorpios feel from the first meeting. What makes this connection uniquely potent is how both partners mirror each other's strengths and vulnerabilities, creating a relationship that's equally challenging and rewarding.\n\nFor these two water signs, emotional connection precedes everything else. They don't just fall in love; they recognize themselves in each other, creating a bond that transcends conventional relationship definitions. This profound recognition explains why Scorpio-Scorpio relationships often feel fated rather than chosen.\n\n**Date Idea:** Plan a night of stargazing in a remote location. Bring a bottle of red wine and prepare for conversations that might last until dawn, exploring topics from personal transformations to universal mysteries.\n\n## Understanding Scorpio Personality Traits\n\nScorpio personalities are among the most complex and intense in the zodiac, driven by deep emotions and a powerful desire for truth. These water signs bring passion and determination to every aspect of their lives, creating both challenges and opportunities in their relationships with others who share their sun sign.\n\n### Common Characteristics of Scorpio Men\n\nScorpio men embody intensity and mystery in their approach to life and relationships. They're fiercely loyal individuals who value honesty and authenticity above all else. Their emotional depth is masked by a controlled exterior, making them appear calm while they process feelings with remarkable thoroughness.\n\nRuled by both Mars and Pluto, Scorpio men possess incredible determination and willpower, approaching their goals with unwavering focus and persistence. They're natural leaders with magnetic charisma that draws others to them, though they carefully select who they allow into their inner circle.\n\nTrust is paramount for the Scorpio man – once broken, it's extremely difficult to rebuild. This protective instinct extends to those they care about, making them formidable defenders of loved ones. In romantic relationships, they seek profound connection rather than superficial interactions, requiring partners who can match their emotional investment and perceptiveness.\n\n### Defining Traits of Scorpio Women\n\nScorpio women combine intuitive intelligence with passionate determination, creating a powerfully magnetic presence. They possess an uncanny ability to see beneath surface appearances, instantly detecting dishonesty or manipulation in others. This intuitive strength gives them exceptional insight into people's motivations and unspoken feelings.\n\nIndependence defines the Scorpio woman's approach to life – she values self-sufficiency and rarely asks for help unless absolutely necessary. Her emotional landscape runs deep, with feelings experienced intensely rather than casually. This depth creates both remarkable capacity for empathy and the potential for emotional complexity.\n\nThe Scorpio woman's loyalty knows few bounds once earned, but crossing her can trigger her legendary protective instincts. She approaches relationships with careful consideration, preferring meaningful connections over casual encounters. In partnerships, she brings passionate devotion alongside expectations of emotional honesty and depth, creating relationships characterized by profound intimacy and understanding.\n\n## Compatibility Factors in a Scorpio-Scorpio Relationship\n\nThe compatibility between two Scorpios creates a relationship unlike any other in the zodiac. This water sign pairing brings together individuals who operate on similar emotional frequencies, creating both powerful harmonies and potential challenges that require navigation.\n\n### Emotional Intensity and Depth\n\nEmotional intensity forms the cornerstone of a Scorpio-Scorpio relationship, creating a connection that's both profound and transformative. When two Scorpios unite, they create an emotional vortex where feelings run deep and nothing remains superficial. Their shared water element gives them an intuitive understanding of emotional currents that other signs might miss completely.\n\nIn intimate moments, two Scorpios experience a level of emotional vulnerability that's rare in other pairings. They recognize and honor each other's need to process feelings thoroughly rather than glossing over difficult emotions. This mutual respect for emotional depth allows them to build a sanctuary where both partners feel safe exploring their most complex feelings.\n\nTheir relationship typically features:\n\n- Passionate exchanges that go beyond physical connection\n- Telepathic understanding of each other's mood shifts\n- Transformative emotional experiences that change both partners\n- Shared appreciation for emotional authenticity over pleasantries\n\nThis emotional attunement creates a bond that often feels karmic or destined. Scorpios approach trust cautiously, recognizing its precious nature and the devastation that follows betrayal. When two Scorpios commit to each other, they create a loyalty pact that's nearly unbreakable.\n\nThe trust between two Scorpios doesn't happen instantly—it evolves through numerous tests and demonstrations of reliability. Their shared investigative nature means they'll both probe beneath surface appearances, seeking evidence of genuine commitment. This mutual vetting process, while sometimes challenging, establishes a relationship built on verified trust rather than blind faith.\n\nKey elements in their trust dynamic include:\n\n- Unwavering loyalty once commitment has been established\n- Deep respect for each other's need for occasional privacy\n- Implicit understanding about relationship boundaries\n- Zero tolerance for dishonesty or manipulation\n\nParadoxically, their mutual possessiveness often strengthens rather than weakens their bond. Two Scorpios recognize and respect each other's territorial nature, understanding that jealousy stems from emotional investment rather than control. This shared trait creates a relationship where both partners feel deeply valued and irreplaceable to each other.\n\n## Communication Patterns Between Two Scorpios\n\nCommunication between two Scorpios operates on multiple levels simultaneously, creating a complex interplay of verbal and non-verbal exchanges. Scorpio pairs develop a unique communication style that reflects their water sign depth and fixed modality persistence.\n\n### The Unspoken Connection\n\nScorpio couples often communicate through intense eye contact, subtle body language shifts, and unspoken emotional cues before words are even necessary. This telepathic connection stems from their shared intuitive abilities and emotional intelligence, allowing them to sense each other's moods and thoughts with remarkable accuracy.\n\nWhen Scorpios do speak to each other, their conversations typically cut through surface pleasantries and dive directly into meaningful topics. They discuss philosophical questions, emotional experiences, and psychological insights with unflinching honesty. Topics other signs might avoid—death, power dynamics, sexuality, and transformation—are regular conversation territory for this pair.\n\nSilence plays an equally important role in Scorpio-Scorpio communication. These two understand that silence isn't emptiness but a space filled with emotional processing. They're comfortable sitting together without speaking, each aware of the internal emotional landscapes being navigated.\n\nText messages and written communication between Scorpios tend to be concise yet loaded with meaning. They excel at conveying significant emotional content in few words, often using private references and inside jokes that strengthen their bond while remaining mysterious to outsiders.\n\n### Navigating Difficult Conversations\n\nArguments between two Scorpios rarely stay superficial. Disagreements quickly reach core issues, with both partners instinctively honing in on underlying vulnerabilities or power imbalances. This intensity can make conflicts particularly challenging but also potentially transformative, as neither partner is willing to settle for shallow resolution.\n\nThe communication style of two Scorpios evolves through distinct phases. Initial conversations feature strategic information sharing as they cautiously reveal themselves. When discussing a significant topic, each partner shares their initial thoughts, then acknowledges the emotions underlying those thoughts, and finally reveals the core needs or fears driving those emotions. This structured approach helps Scorpio couples move beyond power struggles to genuine understanding.\n\n## Challenges in a Scorpio-Scorpio Relationship\n\nWhen two Scorpios unite, their relationship faces unique obstacles stemming from their shared intensity and strong-willed nature. The relationship thrives when both recognize these patterns and establish clear domains of influence, allowing each partner to lead in different aspects of their shared life without feeling diminished.\n\n**⚠️ Relationship Alert:** Power struggles between two Scorpios can become particularly toxic if they evolve into emotional manipulation tactics. [![Scorpios value loyalty, making betrayal a major offense.](https://www.wikihow.com/images/thumb/6/69/Scorpio-Man-Scorpio-Woman-Step-5.jpg/v4-460px-Scorpio-Man-Scorpio-Woman-Step-5.jpg)](https://www.wikihow.com/Scorpio-Man-Scorpio-Woman#/Image:Scorpio-Man-Scorpio-Woman-Step-5.jpg)\n\n**Scorpios value loyalty, making betrayal a major offense.** Because Scorpios are so guarded and mysterious, when they devote themselves to something or someone, they expect loyalty and devotion in return. They’re emotionally intelligent enough to understand the reasons behind betrayal, but as the sign with the rawest nerves in the zodiac, they’re unlikely to forgive disloyalty.\n\n\n- Represented by the scorpion, a Scorpio’s intensity can make them “scary” to other signs, but their cold, dark, intense personas are really just there to defend the ultra-tender hearts underneath.[\\[7\\]](https://www.wikihow.com/Scorpio-Man-Scorpio-Woman#_note-7)X [Expert Source](https://www.wikihow.com/wikiHow:Delivering-a-Trustworthy-Experience) [![Jessica Lanyadoo](https://www.wikihow.com/images/thumb/1/1e/Jessica_Lanyadoo_.png/-crop-100-100-100px-Jessica_Lanyadoo_.png)Jessica Lanyadoo\\\\\n\\\\\nAstrologer & Psychic Medium](https://www.wikihow.com/Author/Jessica-Lanyadoo) Expert Interview\n- **Reader Poll:** We asked 845 wikiHow readers who are Scorpios, and **65%** of them agreed that their biggest dealbreaker is **lying**. [\\[Take Poll\\]](https://www.wikihow.com/Best-Match-for-Scorpio-Man#reader_poll_1765) So to avoid feelings of betrayal in a Scorpio-Scorpio relationship, both partners should always tell the truth—even when it's hard.\n\nAdvertisement\n\nSection 6 of 6:\n\n### Scorpio & Scorpio Potential Challenges\n\n[![PDF download](https://www.wikihow.com/extensions/wikihow/socialstamp/images/icon-pdf.svg)Download Article](https://www.wikihow.com/Scorpio-Man-Scorpio-Woman#)\n\n1. [![Two Scorpios may...](https://www.wikihow.com/images/thumb/b/be/Scorpio-Man-Scorpio-Woman-Step-6.jpg/v4-460px-Scorpio-Man-Scorpio-Woman-Step-6.jpg)](https://www.wikihow.com/Scorpio-Man-Scorpio-Woman#/Image:Scorpio-Man-Scorpio-Woman-Step-6.jpg)\n\n**Two Scorpios may struggle to [**trust**](https://www.wikihow.com/Trust \"Trust\") one another.** Scorpios in love share an intense emotional connection verging on telepathy. They can sense what the other feels and needs, and their loyalty and dedication make them a natural pair. They just need to be sure to abandon their instinct for self-preservation around one another—the instinct that makes them prone to secrecy and stubbornness. A relationship won’t last without vulnerability, trust, and flexibility.\n\n\n- Scorpios in love may also struggle if they become competitive with one another—say, if they’re in the same career field or have the same hobby. As long as they maintain some independence within their relationship, they may [avoid competition](https://www.wikihow.com/Stop-Being-Competitive \"Stop Being Competitive\") with each other.\n\n##
